**Background**
----------------

Phishing is a type of social engineering attack that involves deceiving people, often by creating fake emails, to obtain sensitive information, such as login credentials. Phishing emails aim to deceive victims into revealing the required information, usually by making them believe they are receiving an urgent or legitimate message, like a password reset or technical issue notification.
